;============================================================================
; Faxanadu (U).nes
;
; PRG8 ($8000 - $bfff)
;============================================================================


.segment "PRG8"
.ORG $8000



;============================================================================
; Offsets into the tile data for player sprites, items, and the start screen.
;
; These contain:
;
; 1. Direct references to the start of tile data for a
;    category
;
; 2. Lookup tables mapping a type of an item (e.g., weapon)
;    to the tile IDs based on the start of that category's
;    tile data.
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadArmorSpriteTilesAddr
;============================================================================



;
; Address for the armor-to-tiles offsets lookup table.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadArmorSpriteTilesAddr
;

[8000]TILES_ARMOR_ADDRS_INDEX_REF:; [$8000]
[8000].word $0012; TILES_PLAYER_ARMOR_ADDRS_INDEX [$PRG8::8000]



;
; Address for the weapon-to-tiles offsets lookup table.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadWeaponSpriteTileAddrs
;

[8002]TILES_WEAPON_ADDRS_INDEX_REF:; [$8002]
[8002].word $016b; TILES_PLAYER_WEAPON_ADDRS_INDEX [$PRG8::8002]



;
; Start address of all armor tiles.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadArmorTile
;

[8004]TILES_ARMOR_START_REF:; [$8004]
[8004].word $01a4; SPRITE_TILES_PLAYER_ARMOR_LEATHER_00_WSHIELD_00__STUDDED_00_WSHIELD_00__FULL_PLATE_00_WSHIELD_00 [$PRG8::8004]



;
; Start address of all weapon tiles.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadWeaponTile
;

[8006]TILES_WEAPONS_START_REF:; [$8006]
[8006].word $0a94; TILES_WEAPONS_START_DAGGER_02 [$PRG8::8006]



;
; Start address of common game tiles.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Sprites_LoadCommon
;

[8008]TILES_COMMON_START_REF:; [$8008]
[8008].word $0c04; TILES_COMMON_START [$PRG8::8008]



;
; Start address of all shield tiles.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadShieldTile
;

[800a]TILES_SHIELDS_START_REF:; [$800a]
[800a].word $1104; TILES_SHIELDS_START_SMALL_SHIELD_01 [$PRG8::800a]



;
; Address for the shield-to-tiles offsets lookup table.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     Player_LoadShieldSpriteTileAddrs
;

[800c]TILES_SHIELDS_ADDRS_INDEX_REF:; [$800c]
[800c].word $018c; TILES_SHIELDS_ADDRS_INDEX [$PRG8::800c]



;
; Address for the portrait-to-tiles offsets lookup table.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     IScripts_LoadPortraitTilesAddress
;

[800e]TILES_PORTRAITS_ADDRS_INDEX_REF:; [$800e]
[800e].word $1224; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAITS_ADDRS_INDEX [$PRG8::800e]



;
; Start address for all portrait tiles.
;
;
; XREFS:
;     IScripts_DrawPortraitTileToPPU
;

[8010]TILES_PORTRAITS_START_REF:; [$8010]
[8010].word $136b; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_PINKSHIRT_00 [$PRG8::8010]

;============================================================================
; A mapping of portrait IDs (0-based) to tile address lists.
;
; Each entry in the tile address lists are single-byte
; values that are converted into a 16-bit value
; representing an address in this bank, relative to
; the start of the list of tiles
; (SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_PINKSHIRT_00).
;
; As an example:
;
;     0x8A == $08A0
;           + $936B
;          == $9C0B
;
; A value of 0xFF means tile drawing is done for that
; portrait.
;
; XREFS:
;     TILES_PORTRAITS_ADDRS_INDEX_REF [$PRG8::800e]
;============================================================================



;
; XREFS:
;     TILES_PORTRAITS_ADDRS_INDEX_REF [$PRG8::800e]
;

[9224]SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAITS_ADDRS_INDEX:; [$9224]
[9224].word $123a; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_KING [$PRG8::9224]
[9226].word $1252; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_GURU [$PRG8::9226]
[9228].word $1265; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_MARTIAL_ARTIST [$PRG8::9228]
[922a].word $1285; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_MAGICIAN [$PRG8::922a]
[922c].word $1298; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_DOCTOR [$PRG8::922c]
[922e].word $12b1; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_NURSE [$PRG8::922e]
[9230].word $12cd; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_PINKSHIRT [$PRG8::9230]
[9232].word $12e9; SPRITE_TILES_PORTRAIT_ADDRS_SMOKING_GUY [$PRG8::9232]
